Private Sub AccelerationIssued_DblClick(Cancel As Integer)

   DoCmd.CancelEvent
Else

    End If

Private Sub AddNewDate_Click()
If FileReadOnly Or EditDispute Then
   DoCmd.CancelEvent
Else
    If StatusResults.Value = 1 Then
        StatusHearing.Enabled = True
        StatusHearing.Locked = False
        StatusHearingTime.Enabled = True
        StatusHearingTime.Locked = False
        StatusResults.Value = Null
    End If
            
    If IsNull(StatusResults) Then
        StatusHearing.Enabled = True
        StatusHearing.Locked = False
        StatusHearingTime.Enabled = True
        StatusHearingTime.Locked = False
    End If
End If
  
End Sub

Private Sub AddNewDateException_Click()
If cbxSustained.Value = 4 Then
ExceptionsHearing.Enabled = True
ExceptionsHearing.Locked = False
ExceptionsHearingTime.Enabled = True
ExceptionsHearingTime.Locked = False
cbxSustained.Value = Null
End If
End Sub

Private Sub BidAmount_AfterUpdate()
If Not BHproject Then

    If IsNull(Me.DispositionDesc) And Not IsNull(Sale) And (Date <= Sale Or Format(Date, "mm/dd/yyyy") = Format(Sale, "mm/dd/yyyy")) And Not IsNull(Me.BidReceived) And Not IsNull(BidAmount) Then
    Me.ComEdit.Enabled = True
      '  Me.SalePrice.Locked = False I stopped for the tickt 3296 after talk with Mike, SA 8/2/2018
     '   Me.Purchaser.Locked = False
     '   Me.PurchaserAddress.Locked = False
     '   Me.cmdPurchaserInvestor.Enabled = True
    End If

End If
End Sub

Private Sub cmdAddMonitor_Click()
Dim rs As Recordset
                                                
If Not IsNull(Me.Sale) And Not IsNull(Me.SaleTime) And IsNull(Me.SaleCalendarEntryID) Then
                                                
    Set rs = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * FROM FCDetails where filenumber=" & Me.FileNumber & " and current=true", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
        rs.Edit
        rs!Deposit = Null
        rs!SaleSet = Null
        rs!Disposition = Null
        rs!DispositionDate = Null
        rs!Sale = Null
        rs!SaleTime = Null
        'Forms!Foreclosuredetails!DispositionInitials = Null
        rs.Update
        rs.Close
        Set rs = Nothing
        'Forms!Foreclosuredetails.Requery
        Me.Requery
Else
                                                                                                                                                                             
        If (IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMonitorReferRecd!Monitor_Refer_reced) Or (Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMonitorReferRecd!Monitor_Refer_reced = "")) And (Forms![case list]!CaseTypeID = 8) Or (IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMonitorReferRecd!Monitor_Refer_reced) Or (Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMonitorReferRecd!Monitor_Refer_reced = "")) And (Forms![case list]!CaseTypeID = 1) Then
            Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMonitorReferRecd!Monitor_Refer_reced = Date
        End If
                                                                                                         
                Me!Deposit = Null
                Me!SaleSet = Null
                Me!Disposition = Null
                Me!DispositionDate = Null
                                                                                                                    
            If Not IsNull(Me!Sale) Then
                Me!Sale = Null
                Me!SaleTime = Null
                'Forms!Foreclosuredetails!.Requery
            End If
                                                                                                                      
            Me!Sale.Locked = False
            Me!SaleTime.Locked = False
End If
            'Forms!Foreclosuredetails!.Requery
                                                            
            If Not IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMonitorReferRecd!Monitor_Refer_reced) Then
                AddStatus FileNumber, Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMonitorReferRecd!Monitor_Refer_reced, "Monitor Referral Recieved"
                                                            
                Dim FeeAmt As Currency
                    FeeAmt = Nz(DLookup("MonitorFee", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & Forms![case list]!ClientID))
                    AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-MON", "Monitor sale fee", Format$(FeeAmt, "Currency"), 0, True, True, False, False
            Else
                AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Moitor Referral Removed"
            End If
'End If

End Sub

Private Sub cmdCancel_Click()
Dim i As Integer
Dim sfx As String
Dim rstDox As Recordset

CheckAgain:  Set rstDox = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * from DocIndexOpen where  FileNumber =" & FileNumber & " And StaffID = " & GetStaffID & " And Filespec Is Not Null ", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
If Not rstDox.EOF Then

    If IsFileOpen(rstDox!Filespec, FileNumber, rstDox!StaffID) Then
    MsgBox (rstDox!Filespec & " is still open, please close it ")
    rstDox.Close
    Set rstDox = Nothing
    Exit Sub
    Else
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("DELETE from docIndexOpen WHERE  FileNumber =" & FileNumber & " And StaffID = " & GetStaffID & " And Filespec ='" & rstDox!Filespec & "'")
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
    GoTo CheckAgain
    End If

End If
rstDox.Close
Set rstDox = Nothing

DoCmd.OpenForm ("GetProcessServerCancelInfo")
End Sub

Else

End If
    
End Sub

Dim i As Integer
Dim rs, rs1 As Recordset
Dim mystring As String

mystring = ""

DoCmd.SetWarnings False
DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE Staff set DCSelected = false where DCSelected = true")

DoCmd.RunSQL "delete * from DC_CompSelectedAtty where Filenumber = " & Forms![case list]!FileNumber
DoCmd.SetWarnings True
            
Set rs1 = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("select * from DC_CompSelectedAtty", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
'Set rs = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("select * from staff where PracticeDC = true and Active = true", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)

For i = 0 To lstDCAtty.ListCount - 1

Set rs = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("select * from staff where Id = " & Me.lstDCAtty.Column(0, i), dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
    If lstDCAtty.Selected(i) Then

'    Dim t As Integer
'    t = Val(Me.lstDCAtty.Column(0, i))
'    'DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE Staff set selected = 1 where Id = " & Val(Me.lstDCAtty.Column(0, i)))
'    DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE Staff set Selected = 1 where Id = " & t)

        rs1.AddNew
        rs1!FileNumber = Forms![case list]!FileNumber
        rs1!AttyID = Me.lstDCAtty.Column(0, i)
        rs1!Name = rs!Name
        rs1!EMail = rs!EMail
        rs1!DCBar = rs!DCBar

        
        rs1.Update
        
        If mystring = "" Then
            mystring = Me.lstDCAtty.Column(1, i)
        Else
            mystring = mystring & ", " & Me.lstDCAtty.Column(1, i)
        End If
    
    End If
    Next i

    rs1.Close
    Set rs1 = Nothing
    rs.Close
    Set rs = Nothing
    
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    DoCmd.OpenQuery ("SetDCAtty")
    'DoCmd.SetWarnings True
    
    
    strInfo = "List of DC Attorney selected: " & mystring & ""
    strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
    strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
    DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
    Forms!Journal.Requery

 'cmdConfirm.Enabled = False

Private Sub cmdDocstoClient_Click()
If Not IsNull(DocstoClient) Then
    
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!DocstoClient.Locked = False

    DocstoClient = ""
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!DocstoClient.Locked = True


    If Not IsNull(DocsBack) Then
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "removed docs to client field and All Docs Received date"
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    Else
    
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "removed docs to client field"
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery

    End If
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE WizardSupportTwo set LimboWhit = null ,LimboYellow = null ,LimboRed = null WHERE FileNumber = " & Me.FileNumber & " and current = true")
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
End If

If Not IsNull(DocsBack) Then
    DocsBack = ""
End If

If DCount("*", "FCdetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber) > 1 Then
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE WizardQueueStats set RestartComplete  = null WHERE FileNumber = " & Me.FileNumber & " and current = true")
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
End If


End Sub

Private Sub cmdRemoveDisposition_Click()

   Exit Sub
End If

Exit Sub
End If

Me.Disposition = Null
Me.DispositionDate = Null
Me.DispositionStaffID = Null

strInfo = "Dispostion Removed"

Forms.Journal.Requery


AddStatus FileNumber, Now, "Dispositon Removed"


End If






End Sub

Private Sub CmdRequestTitle_Click()
If Forms![case list].Active = False Then
MsgBox ("File is inactive")
Exit Sub


Else


    If Not IsNull(Me.Disposition) Then
    Select Case Me.Disposition
        Case 11, 1, 7, 2, 30
             DoCmd.OpenForm ("EnterRequestTitleOrderReason")
             Forms!EnterRequestTitleOrderReason.FileNumber = Me.FileNumber
        Case Else
            MsgBox ("There is dispostion, the file will not go Title Order Queue")
            Exit Sub
        End Select
    Else
    DoCmd.OpenForm ("EnterRequestTitleOrderReason")
    Forms!EnterRequestTitleOrderReason.FileNumber = Me.FileNumber
    End If
End If



   


End Sub

CheckAgain:  Set rstDox = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * from DocIndexOpen where  FileNumber =" & FileNumber & " And StaffID = " & GetStaffID & " And Filespec Is Not Null ", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
If Not rstDox.EOF Then

    If IsFileOpen(rstDox!Filespec, FileNumber, rstDox!StaffID) Then
    MsgBox (rstDox!Filespec & " is still open, please close it ")
    rstDox.Close
    Set rstDox = Nothing
    Exit Sub
    Else
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("DELETE from docIndexOpen WHERE  FileNumber =" & FileNumber & " And StaffID = " & GetStaffID & " And Filespec ='" & rstDox!Filespec & "'")
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
    GoTo CheckAgain
    End If

End If
rstDox.Close
Set rstDox = Nothing

Dim rstCase As Recordset, rstFC As Recordset, rstNames As Recordset
Dim rstsale As Recordset

Dim FileNum As Long, MissingTxt As String

On Error GoTo Err_cmdOK_Click

Select Case WizardSource

Exit Sub

    Set rstvalumeintake = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * from ValumeRestart", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
    With rstvalumeintake
    .AddNew
    !CaseFile = FileNumber
    !Client = DLookup("ShortClientName", "ClientList", "ClientID = " & Forms![case list]!ClientID)
    !RestartComplete = Now
    !RestartCompleteC = 1
 
    !Name = GetFullName()
    .Update
    End With
    Set rstvalumeintake = Nothing

    Dim lrs As Recordset
    Set lrs = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("select * from journal where FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND warning = 100", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
    With lrs
    '.Edit
    Do Until .EOF
    .Edit
    ![Warning] = 0
    .Update
    .MoveNext
    
    Loop
    '.Update
    End With

    rstsql = "Insert into ValuemDispo (CaseFile, Client, PrimaryDefName, State, Disposition, DispoQCompleted, Name ) values (" & Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber & ",'" & ClientShortName(Forms![case list]!ClientID) & "','" & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & "', '" & Forms!ForeclosureDetails!State & "'," & Me.Disposition & ", # " & Now() & " #,'" & GetFullName() & "') "
    DoCmd.RunSQL rstsql
    rstsql = ""
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True

    Call ReleaseFile(FileNumber)
    MsgBox "Dispo Wizard Completed", vbInformation
    DoCmd.Close acForm, "Journal"
    DoCmd.Close acForm, "ForeclosureDetails"
    DoCmd.Close acForm, "Case List"

Case "FeeRequest"

    DoCmd.SetWarnings False

    DoCmd.OpenQuery ("MK_Temp_FeeCostApp")
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("DELETE from Temp_FeeCostApp")

    rstsql = "Insert into Temp_FeeCostApp select * from FeeRequested where Filenumber = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber and (StatusID is null or StatusID = 4) and ReqDate is null"
    'rstsql = "Insert into Temp_FeeCostApp select * from FeeRequested where (Filenumber = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber and (StatusID is null or StatusID = 4) and ReqDate is null) or (Filenumber = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber and StatusID = 2)"
    DoCmd.RunSQL rstsql
    rstsql = ""

    DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE Temp_FeeCostApp SET Type = 'Fee'")

    rstsql = "Insert into Temp_FeeCostApp select * from CostRequested where Filenumber = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber and (StatusID is null or StatusID = 4) and ReqDate is null"
    'rstsql = "Insert into Temp_FeeCostApp select * from CostRequested where (Filenumber = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber and (StatusID is null or StatusID = 4) and ReqDate is null) or (Filenumber = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber and StatusID = 2) "

    DoCmd.RunSQL rstsql
    rstsql = ""
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE Temp_FeeCostApp SET Type = 'Cost'where isnull(type) = true")
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True

    DoCmd.OpenForm ("SetApprovalFeesCosts")

Case "FeeApproval"

    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    
    DoCmd.OpenQuery ("MK_Temp_StatusFeeCostApp")
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("DELETE from Temp_FeeCostStatusApp")
    
    rstsql = "Insert into Temp_FeeCostStatusApp select * from FeeRequested where Filenumber = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber and StatusID is null and ReqDate is not null"
    DoCmd.RunSQL rstsql
    rstsql = ""
    
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE Temp_FeeCostStatusApp SET Type = 'Fee'")
    
    rstsql = "Insert into Temp_FeeCostStatusApp select * from CostRequested where Filenumber = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber and StatusID is null and ReqDate is not null"
    DoCmd.RunSQL rstsql
    rstsql = ""
    
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE Temp_FeeCostStatusApp SET Type = 'Cost'where isnull(type) = true")
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True

    DoCmd.OpenForm ("SetApprovalStatusFeesCosts")


End Select

Exit_cmdOK_Click:
    Exit Sub

Err_cmdOK_Click:
    MsgBox Err.Description
    Resume Exit_cmdOK_Click
    
End Sub

Dim rstDox As Recordset

    MsgBox (rstDox!Filespec & " is still open, please close it ")
    rstDox.Close
    Set rstDox = Nothing
    Exit Sub
    Else
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("DELETE from docIndexOpen WHERE  FileNumber =" & FileNumber & " And StaffID = " & GetStaffID & " And Filespec ='" & rstDox!Filespec & "'")

    End If

Private Sub AuditFile_AfterUpdate()
AddStatus FileNumber, AuditFile, "Audit filed"
End Sub

Private Sub AuditFile_BeforeUpdate(Cancel As Integer)
If Not BHproject Then
Cancel = CheckFutureDate(AuditFile)
End If

End Sub

Private Sub AuditFile_DblClick(Cancel As Integer)
If FileReadOnly Or EditDispute Or IsNull(Disposition) Or (Disposition <> 1 And Disposition <> 2) Then
   DoCmd.CancelEvent
Else
    AuditFile = Now()
    AddStatus FileNumber, AuditFile, "Audit filed"
End If

End Sub

AddStatus FileNumber, AuditRat, "Audit ratified"
End Sub

If Not BHproject Then
Cancel = CheckFutureDate(AuditRat)
End If

End Sub

Private Sub AuditRat_DblClick(Cancel As Integer)
If FileReadOnly Or EditDispute Or IsNull(Disposition) Or (Disposition <> 1 And Disposition <> 2) Then
   DoCmd.CancelEvent
Else
    AuditRat = Now()
    AddStatus FileNumber, AuditRat, "Audit ratified"
End If

End Sub

Private Sub BidReceived_AfterUpdate()
If BHproject Then
AddStatus FileNumber, BidReceived, "Bid received"
Else

AddStatus FileNumber, BidReceived, "Bid received"
If IsNull(Me.DispositionDesc) And Not IsNull(Sale) And (Date <= Sale Or Format(Date, "mm/dd/yyyy") = Format(Sale, "mm/dd/yyyy")) And Not IsNull(Me.BidReceived) And Not IsNull(BidAmount) Then
    Me.SalePrice.Locked = False
    Me.Purchaser.Locked = False
    Me.PurchaserAddress.Locked = False
    Me.cmdPurchaserInvestor.Enabled = True
End If
End If

End Sub

Private Sub BidReceived_BeforeUpdate(Cancel As Integer)
If Not BHproject Then
  Cancel = CheckFutureDate(BidReceived)
End If

End Sub

Private Sub BidReceived_DblClick(Cancel As Integer)
If FileReadOnly Or EditDispute Then
   DoCmd.CancelEvent
Else
    BidReceived = Date
    AddStatus FileNumber, BidReceived, "Bid received"
End If
End Sub

Private Sub BorrowerServed_AfterUpdate()

If BHproject Then
    AddStatus FileNumber, BorrowerServed, "Borrower served by posting"
Else
    If Not IsNull(BorrowerServed) Then

        AddStatus FileNumber, BorrowerServed, "Borrower served"
    
        Dim rstJnl As Recordset, Comment As String, FeeAmount As Currency
        
'Milestone Billing for Referral Fee
        Dim InvPct As Double
        If State = "MD" Then
    
            If Forms![case list]!ClientID = 634 Then
                FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & Forms![case list]!ClientID))
            Else
    
              Select Case LoanType
              Case 1 'Conventional
                FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & Forms![case list]!ClientID))
              Case 2 'VA or Veteran's Affairs
                FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=573")) 'Veteran's Affairs
              Case 3 'FHA or HUD
                FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=570")) 'HUD/FHA
              Case 4
                FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=177")) 'Fannie Mae
              Case 5
                FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=263")) 'Freddie Mac
              Case Else
                FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & Forms![case list]!ClientID))
                End Select
            End If
        
        
            If (Nz(DLookup("MilestoneBilling", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & Forms![case list]!ClientID))) = -1 Then
                If LoanType = 4 And Forms![case list]!ClientID <> 634 Then
                    InvPct = DLookup("MDservicecomppct", "clientlist", "clientid= 177")
                Else
                    InvPct = DLookup("MDservicecomppct", "clientlist", "clientid=" & Forms![case list]!ClientID)
                End If
        'End If
            End If
            If FeeAmount > 0 And InvPct > 0 Then
                'InvPct = DLookup("MDservicecomppct", "clientlist", "clientid=" & Forms![Case List]!ClientID)
                'If InvPct < 1 Then
                    If LoanType = 4 And Forms![case list]!ClientID <> 634 Then
                        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "FNMA Attorney Fee- " & Format(InvPct, "percent") & " earned at borrower served of " & Format(FeeAmount, "currency"), InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
                    Else
                        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "Attorney Fee- " & Format(InvPct, "percent") & " earned at borrower served of " & Format(FeeAmount, "currency"), InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
    
                    End If
                
                'Else
                    'AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "Attorney Fee", InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
            End If
            
             
            If Not IsNull(BorrowerServed) And (Nz(DLookup("MilestoneBilling", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & Forms![case list]!ClientID))) = -1 And FeeAmount > 0 And InvPct > 0 Then
                
                Forms![case list]!BillCase = True
                Forms![case list]!BillCaseUpdateUser = GetStaffID()
                Forms![case list]!BillCaseUpdateDate = Date
                Forms![case list]![BillCaseUpdateReasonID] = 5
                Forms![case list]!lblBilling.Visible = True
                Forms![case list].SetFocus
                DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord
                Forms![ForeclosureDetails].SetFocus
                
                Dim rstBillReasons As Recordset
                Set rstBillReasons = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * FROM BillingReasonsFCarchive where filenumber=" & FileNumber, dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
                With rstBillReasons
                .AddNew
                !FileNumber = FileNumber
                !BillingReasonID = 5
                !UserID = GetStaffID
                !Date = BorrowerServed
                .Update
                End With
            End If
        
'End If

'End If

DoCmd.OpenForm "GetBorrowerServedFee", , , , , acDialog, "Enter costs for Process Server|FC-PS|Estimated Process Server Costs|Process Server"
'FeeAmount = InputBox("Please re-enter costs for Process Server")

Private Sub BorrowerServed_BeforeUpdate(Cancel As Integer)
If Not BHproject Then
  Cancel = CheckFutureDate(BorrowerServed)
  If (Cancel = 1) Then Exit Sub
  
  If (DateDiff("d", Docket, BorrowerServed) < 0) Then
    Cancel = 1
    MsgBox "Date cannot be before Docket Date.", vbCritical
  End If
End If

End Sub

Private Sub BorrowerServed_DblClick(Cancel As Integer)

If FileReadOnly Or IsNull(ServiceSent) Then
   DoCmd.CancelEvent
ElseIf (Me.WizardSource = "None" And Me.State = "MD") Or (Me.State = "MD" And Len(Me.WizardSource & "") = 0) Then
    DoCmd.CancelEvent
Else
    BorrowerServed = Now()
    AddStatus FileNumber, BorrowerServed, "Borrower served"
    Call BorrowerServed_AfterUpdate
End If

If EditDispute And Not IsNull(Me.ServiceSent) Then
        Me.BorrowerServed.Locked = False
        BorrowerServed = Now()
    AddStatus FileNumber, BorrowerServed, "Borrower served"
    Call BorrowerServed_AfterUpdate
End If

End Sub

Private Sub cbxAddTrustee_AfterUpdate()
Dim t As Recordset

On Error GoTo Err_cbxAddTrustee

Set t = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Trustees", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
t.AddNew
t!FileNumber = Me!FileNumber
t!Trustee = Me!cbxAddTrustee
t!Name = Me!cbxAddTrustee.Column(1)
t!Assigned = Now()

t.Update
t.Close
Me!lstTrustees.Requery
TrusteeWordFile = 0         ' invalidate cache

Exit_cbxAddTrustee:
    Exit Sub

Err_cbxAddTrustee:
    MsgBox Err.Description
    Resume Exit_cbxAddTrustee

End Sub

Private Sub cmdEditPropertyDetails_Click()
On Error GoTo Err_EditPropertyDetails_Click


    Dim stDocName As String
    Dim stLinkCriteria As String

    stDocName = "EditPropertyDetails"
    DoCmd.OpenForm stDocName, , , stLinkCriteria
    With Forms!EditPropertyDetails
        .txtFileNumber = FileNumber
        .PrimaryFirstName = PrimaryFirstName
        .PrimaryLastName = PrimaryLastName
        .SecondaryFirstName = SecondaryFirstName
        .SecondaryLastName = SecondaryLastName
        .PropertyAddress = PropertyAddress
        .City = City
        .State = State
        .ZipCode = ZipCode
        .CourtCaseNumber = CourtCaseNumber
        .TaxID = TaxID
        .Apt = [Fair Debt]
        .optLeasehold = optLeasehold
        .GroundRentAmount = GroundRentAmount
        .GroundRentPayable = GroundRentPayable
    End With

Exit_EditPropertyDetails_Click:
    Exit Sub

Err_EditPropertyDetails_Click:
    MsgBox Err.Description
    Resume Exit_EditPropertyDetails_Click
End Sub

Private Sub Comment_AfterUpdate()
If (IsNull(sComment) Or sComment = "") And Not IsNull(Comment) And Me.sfrmFCtitle.Form!txtComment = "" Or IsNull(Me.sfrmFCtitle.Form!txtComment) Then
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        DoCmd.RunSQL "update FCTitle set comment = '" & Comment & "' where FileNumber = " & Forms![case list]!FileNumber
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Me!sfrmFCtitle.Form.Requery
End If
End Sub


Private Sub ComPraper_Click()
''Check for document Docket packet id = 97  -Sarab 2-3-2016
Dim Filespec As String, newfilename As String
Dim rstDoc As Recordset
Dim rstqueueCount As Integer
Dim objCAcroPDDocDestination As Acrobat.CAcroPDDoc
Dim objCAcroPDDocSource As Acrobat.CAcroPDDoc
Dim GetDocketPaket As Recordset
Dim DocketPaketID As String
Dim strsql As String
Dim strSQLValues As String
Dim GetDicketPaketName As String
Dim GroupCode As String
 GroupCode = ""
Forms!ForeclosureDetails!cmdWizComplete.Enabled = True
        
  'profe = 812
  'source = 1270 'Process Service Cover
  'docket = 97




Set GetDocketPaket = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM DocIndex  WHERE DocTitleID = 97 And FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Filespec IS NOT NULL and DeleteDate is null ORDER BY Datestamp DESC ", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
    If Not GetDocketPaket.EOF Then
        DocketPaketID = GetDocketPaket!DocTitleID
        GetDicketPaketName = GetDocketPaket!Filespec
        Call AffadavitOfService(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber)
        newfilename = "Process Service Cover Sheet"
        DoCmd.OutputTo acOutputReport, "Process Service Cover", acFormatPDF, DocLocation & DocBucket(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber) & "\" & Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber & "\" & newfilename & ".pdf", False, "", 0
        newfilename = "Process Service Cover Sheet" & ".pdf"
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    Else
        MsgBox ("There is no docket Paket document")
        Exit Sub
     End If
Set GetDocketPaket = Nothing
    
   
Set objCAcroPDDocDestination = CreateObject("AcroExch.PDDoc")
Set objCAcroPDDocSource = CreateObject("AcroExch.PDDoc")

        objCAcroPDDocDestination.Open DocLocation & DocBucket(FileNumber) & "\" & FileNumber & "\" & newfilename
        objCAcroPDDocSource.Open DocLocation & DocBucket(FileNumber) & "\" & FileNumber & "\" & GetDicketPaketName
            If Not objCAcroPDDocDestination.InsertPages(objCAcroPDDocDestination.GetNumPages - 1, objCAcroPDDocSource, 0, objCAcroPDDocSource.GetNumPages, 0) Then
                MsgBox (" Error in selected documents")
                objCAcroPDDocSource.Close
                Exit Sub
            End If
        objCAcroPDDocSource.Close
     
        newfilename = "Proof of Service" & " " & Format$(Now(), "yyyymmdd hhnnss") & ".pdf"
        objCAcroPDDocDestination.Save 1, DocLocation & DocBucket(FileNumber) & "\" & FileNumber & "\" & newfilename
        objCAcroPDDocDestination.Close
Set objCAcroPDDocSource = Nothing
Set objCAcroPDDocDestination = Nothing

DoCmd.SetWarnings False

strsql = ""
strSQLValues = FileNumber & "," & 812 & ",'" & GroupCode & "'," & GetStaffID() & ",#" & Now() & "#,'" & Replace(newfilename, "'", "''") & "','" & Replace(newfilename, "'", "''") & "'"
strsql = "Insert Into DocIndex (FileNumber,DocTitleID,DocGroup,StaffID,DateStamp,Filespec,Notes) VALUES (" & strSQLValues & ")"
DoCmd.RunSQL (strsql)
DoCmd.SetWarnings True

StartDoc DocLocation & DocBucket(FileNumber) & "\" & FileNumber & "\" & newfilename





End Sub

Private Sub ComRemoveCase_Click()

If Me.CourtCaseNumber = "" Then
    MsgBox ("There is no case court number")
    Exit Sub
End If
'If Me.State = "MD" Then
'    If IsNull(Me.Disposition) Then
'    MsgBox ("Must enter dispostion first")
'    Exit Sub
'    Else

CaseNuUpdate = True
Dim DResut As Integer
Dim DHresut As Integer

DResut = IIf(IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmDeedRecord!DeferResultID), Nz(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmDeedRecord!DeferResultID), Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmDeedRecord!DeferResultID)
DHresut = IIf(IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmDeedRecord!DeferHearingResults), Nz(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmDeedRecord!DeferHearingResults), (Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmDeedRecord!DeferHearingResults))
    
If Not IsNull(DismissalDate) Or DResut = 3 Or DHresut = 2 Then
    
    If MsgBox("Do you want to remove the case number and all fields for this sale? ", vbYesNo) = vbYes Then

    Call RemoveCaseFiled

    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
'                strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!ForeclosureDetails.FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & "Removed Court Case Number: " & CourtCaseNumber.OldValue & ". " & "',1 )"
'                DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
    strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!ForeclosureDetails.FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & "Case:  " & CourtCaseNumber.oldvalue & " Dismissed. Dates associated with this case have been removed from the file. " & "',1 )"
    DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
    Forms!Journal.Requery

'    DoCmd.Close

    End If

Else
    
            MsgBox ("Case is not yet dismissed on post sale tab")
    End If

End Sub

Private Sub DeedAppFolio_AfterUpdate()
   Dim Folio_Old As String
If Not IsNull(DeedAppFolio.oldvalue) Or DeedAppFolio.oldvalue <> "" Then
    Folio_Old = DeedAppFolio.oldvalue
Else
    Folio_Old = ""
End If

    If IsNull(DeedAppFolio) = False Then
    
        If Folio_Old <> "" Then
            AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Substitution of Trustee Folio changed from " & Folio_Old & " to " & DeedAppFolio & " "
        Else
            AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Substitution of Trustee Folio " & DeedAppFolio & " Entered"
        End If
        
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        
       If Folio_Old <> "" Then
            strInfo = "Substitution of Trustee Folio changed from " & Folio_Old & " to " & DeedAppFolio & ""
       Else
            strInfo = "Substitution of Trustee Folio " & DeedAppFolio & " Entered"
       End If
        
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    Else
        
        If Folio_Old <> "" Then
            AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Removed Substitution of Trustee Folio " & Folio_Old & " "
            
            DoCmd.SetWarnings False
            strInfo = "Removed Substitution of Trustee Folio " & Folio_Old & " "
            strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
            strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
            DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
            DoCmd.SetWarnings True
            Forms!Journal.Requery
        End If
    End If
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmStatus.Requery

End Sub

Private Sub DeedAppLiber_AfterUpdate()
   Dim Liber_Old As String

If IsNull(DeedAppLiber.oldvalue) Or DeedAppLiber.oldvalue = "" Then
    Liber_Old = ""
Else
    Liber_Old = DeedAppLiber.oldvalue
End If
    
    If IsNull(DeedAppLiber) = False Then
    
        If Liber_Old <> "" Then
            AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Substitution of Trustee Liber changed from " & Liber_Old & " to " & DeedAppLiber & " "

        Else
            AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Substitution of Trustee Liber " & DeedAppLiber & " Entered"
        End If
        
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        
        If Liber_Old <> "" Then
            strInfo = "Substitution of Trustee Liber changed from " & Liber_Old & " to " & DeedAppLiber & " "

        Else
            strInfo = "Substitution of Trustee Liber " & DeedAppLiber & " Entered"
        End If
        
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    Else
        If Liber_Old <> "" Then
            AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Removed Substitution of Trustee Liber " & Liber_Old & ""
            
            DoCmd.SetWarnings False
            strInfo = "Removed Substitution of Trustee Liber " & Liber_Old & " "
            strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
            strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"

    End If
    
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmStatus.Requery

End Sub

Private Sub DeedAppReceived_AfterUpdate()
    If IsNull(DeedAppReceived) = False Then
        Me.DocBackDOA = True
        AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Received Substitution of Trustee"
               
        Dim clientShor As String
        Dim strInsert As String
        clientShor = DLookup("ShortClientName", "ClientList", "ClientID= " & Forms![case list]!ClientID)
        clientShor = Replace(clientShor, "'", "''")
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInsert = "Insert Into TrackingSOTreceived (CaseFile,ProjectName,ClientShortName,Client,DIT,DeedAppReceived,StaffID,StaffName,state) Values (" & FileNumber & ",'" & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & "','" & clientShor & "', " & Forms![case list]!ClientID & ", #" & Now() & "#,#" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!DeedAppReceived & "#, " & GetStaffID & ",'" & GetFullName() & "','" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!State & "')"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strInsert
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        clientShor = ""
        strInsert = ""
                    
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Received Substitution of Trustee by " & GetFullName
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    
    Else
        Me.DocBackDOA = False
        AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Removed Substitution of Trustee"
        
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Removed Substitution of Trustee by " & GetFullName
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    End If
End Sub

Private Sub DeedAppRecorded_AfterUpdate()

Dim Date_Old As String

If Not IsNull(DeedAppRecorded.oldvalue) Or DeedAppRecorded.oldvalue <> "" Then
    Date_Old = DeedAppRecorded.oldvalue
Else
    Date_Old = ""
End If

If IsNull(DeedAppRecorded) = False Then

    If Date_Old <> "" Then
    
        AddStatus FileNumber, DeedAppRecorded, "Substitution of Trustee Recorded date changed from " & Date_Old & " to " & DeedAppRecorded & ""
    
    Else
        AddStatus FileNumber, DeedAppRecorded, "Substitution of Trustee Recorded "
    End If
    
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    
    If Date_Old <> "" Then
        strInfo = "Substitution of Trustee Recorded date changed from " & Date_Old & " to " & DeedAppRecorded & ""
    Else
        strInfo = "Substitution of Trustee Recorded "
    End If
    
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
 Else
    If Date_Old <> "" Then
        AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Removed Substitution of Trustee Recorded date " & Date_Old & " "
       
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Removed Substitution of Trustee Recorded date " & Date_Old & " "
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    End If
End If
Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmStatus.Requery

Private Sub Deposit_AfterUpdate()

'Added on 10_17_16

Dim jouralStr As String
 
 If (Not IsNull(Deposit.oldvalue) Or Deposit.oldvalue > 0) And (IsNull(Deposit) Or Deposit = 0) Then
    jouralStr = "Deposit amount removed"
 ElseIf (Not IsNull(Deposit.oldvalue) Or Deposit.oldvalue > 0) And (Not IsNull(Deposit) Or Deposit > 0) And Deposit.oldvalue <> Deposit Then
    jouralStr = "Deposit amount edited from " & Deposit.oldvalue & " to " & Deposit & ""
 ElseIf (IsNull(Deposit.oldvalue) Or Deposit.oldvalue = 0) And (Not IsNull(Deposit) Or Deposit > 0) Then
    jouralStr = "Added Deposit amount " & Deposit & ""
 End If
 If jouralStr <> "" Then
  'Forms!foreclosuredetails.Requery

    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
       strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & jouralStr & "',1 )"
       DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
    Forms!Journal.Requery
End If

End Sub

Private Sub DocBackLossMitFinal_AfterUpdate()

If Me.Dirty Then DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord

If DocBackLossMitFinal Then
    AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Received FLMA"
    
    If Not DocBackLossMitFinal Then
           DocBackLossMitFinal = True
        If Me.Dirty Then DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord
    End If
Else
    AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Removed FLMA"
    
    If DocBackLossMitFinal Then
        DocBackLossMitFinal = False
        If Me.Dirty Then DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord
    End If
End If

End Sub

Private Sub ExceptionsHearing_BeforeUpdate(Cancel As Integer)



If Not BHproject Then
    If Not ExceptionsFiled Then
        MsgBox " Check the Exceptions Filed box"
        Me.Undo
        
        Exit Sub
        Else
            If HearingCheking(ExceptionsHearing, 1) = 1 Then
                Cancel = 1
            End If
        
            If Weekday(ExceptionsHearing) = vbSunday Or Weekday(ExceptionsHearing) = vbSaturday Then
                
                MsgBox "Exceptions Hearing date cannot be Saturday or Sunday", vbCritical
               Cancel = 1
            End If
    
    End If
End If



End Sub

Private Sub ExceptionsHearingTime_AfterUpdate()
If Not BHproject Then
    If IsNull(ExceptionsHearing) Or IsNull(ExceptionsHearingTime) Then Exit Sub
    
'    If Hour(ExceptionsHearingTime) < 8 Or Hour(ExceptionsHearingTime) > 18 Then
'        ExceptionsHearingTime = DateAdd("h", 12, ExceptionsHearingTime)
'        If Hour(ExceptionsHearingTime) < 8 Or Hour(ExceptionsHearingTime) > 18 Then
'            MsgBox "Invalid Exceptions Hearing time: " & Format$(ExceptionsHearingTime, "h:nn am/pm")
'            ExceptionsHearingTime = Null
'            Exit Sub
'        End If
'    End If

'edited on 9/8/15
    If Hour(ExceptionsHearingTime) >= 8 And Hour(ExceptionsHearingTime) < 13 Then
            ExceptionsHearingTime = Format$(ExceptionsHearingTime, "h:nn am/pm")
    ElseIf Hour(ExceptionsHearingTime) >= 1 And Hour(ExceptionsHearingTime) <= 6 Then
            ExceptionsHearingTime = DateAdd("h", 12, ExceptionsHearingTime)
    Else
            MsgBox "Hearing time must be between 8:00 AM and 6:00 PM" ': " & Format$(DCHearingTime, "h:nn am/pm")
            ExceptionsHearingTime = Null
            Exit Sub
    End If
    
    AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Exceptions Hearing scheduled time for " & Format$(ExceptionsHearing, "m/d/yyyy") & " at " & Format$(ExceptionsHearingTime, "h:nn am/pm")
    If Not IsNull(ExceptionsHearing) Then Call UpdateCalendarExceptionHearing
    Call Visuals
    ExceptionsHearingTime.Locked = True
End If

End Sub

If FileReadOnly Or EditDispute Or IsNull(Disposition) Or (Disposition <> 1 And Disposition <> 2) Then
   DoCmd.CancelEvent
End If
End Sub

Private Sub Form_Load()
If Len(Me.OpenArgs) > 0 Then
If Me.OpenArgs = "Title" Or Me.OpenArgs = "titleNew" Then
 Me.TitleBack.BackColor = vbYellow
 Me.TitleOrder.BackColor = vbYellow
 Me.TitleThru.BackColor = vbYellow
 cmdWaiting.Caption = "TITLE"
 Forms!ForeclosureDetails!cmdWaiting.FontBold = True
Forms!ForeclosureDetails!cmdWaiting.ForeColor = vbBlack

 Else
    If Me.OpenArgs = "TitleOut" Then
    Me.TitleBack.BackColor = vbGreen
    Me.TitleOrder.BackColor = vbGreen
    Me.TitleThru.BackColor = vbGreen
    cmdWaiting.Caption = "TITLE Outstanding"
    Else
    
 Me.TitleBack.BackColor = vbWhite
 Me.TitleOrder.BackColor = vbWhite
 Me.TitleThru.BackColor = vbWhite
 cmdWaiting.Caption = "Waiting for Restart"
 'Waiting for Restart
 
 End If
 End If
 End If

 sComment = Nz(Me.Comment)
 
' If DLookup("Filenumber", "TitleClaimFeeApprovoed ", "Filenumber = " & FileNumber) > 0 Then
'   If TitleFee = False Then
'
'    DoCmd.SetWarnings False

'    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
'
'   End If
'End If

End Sub

'[pre-sale].Enabled = False
End If


'Sarab10/16 Michael this is the loop that might messup with the staff.

Private Sub New45Notice_Click()

If (IsNull(Disposition) Or (Disposition = 1 Or Disposition = 2)) Then

    If Not IsNull([NOI]) Or ([ClientSentNOI] = "C") Then
    
    If MsgBox(" You are about to remove dates ? ", vbOKCancel) = vbOK Then
    
        '45 Day Notice sent
        AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Removed 45 Days Notice (" & [NOI] & ") by " & GetFullName
    
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Removed 45 Days Notice (" & [NOI] & ") by " & GetFullName
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    
        'Put file in FairDebt queue
        Dim rstNOI As Recordset
        Set rstNOI = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * From WizardQueueStats Where FileNumber = " & FileNumber & "And Current = True", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
            If Not rstNOI.EOF Then
                With rstNOI
                .Edit
               ' If IsNull(!FairDebtComplete) Then !FairDebtComplete = #1/2/2012# NOICompleteDocsMsng
                !NOIcomplete = Null
                !DateInWaiitingQueueNOI = Null
                !DateInQueueNOI = Null
               ' !Add45 = "45day"
                .Update
                End With
                Else
                MsgBox ("There is no Currrent Wizard Record for this File, Please Contact the IT")
            End If
        Set rstNOI = Nothing
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails![NOI] = Null
        
                  
            If Forms!ForeclosureDetails!txtClientSentNOI = "C" Then
                AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Removed C Of NOI by " & GetFullName
                
                DoCmd.SetWarnings False
                strInfo = "Removed C Of NOI by " & GetFullName
                strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
                strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
                DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
                DoCmd.SetWarnings True
                Forms!Journal.Requery
            
                Forms!ForeclosureDetails!txtClientSentNOI = ""
            End If
    
    End If
    Else
    Exit Sub
    End If
Else
MsgBox ("The File has dispsotion not buy in or 3rd party, proceduer canceld")
Exit Sub
End If


End Sub

Private Sub NewDemand_Click()

If (IsNull(Disposition) Or (Disposition = 1 Or Disposition = 2)) Then

    If Not IsNull([AccelerationIssued]) Or Not IsNull([AccelerationLetter]) Or ([ClientSentAcceleration] = "C") Then
        If MsgBox(" You are about to remove dates ? ", vbOKCancel) = vbOK Then
        
            AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Removed Demand Issued (" & [AccelerationIssued] & ") by " & GetFullName
        
            DoCmd.SetWarnings False
            strInfo = "Removed Demand Issued (" & [AccelerationIssued] & ") by " & GetFullName
            strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
            strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
            DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
            DoCmd.SetWarnings True
            Forms!Journal.Requery
        
            'Put file in Demand queue
            Dim rstAccelerationIssued As Recordset
            Set rstAccelerationIssued = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * From WizardQueueStats Where FileNumber = " & FileNumber & "And Current = True", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
                If Not rstAccelerationIssued.EOF Then
                    With rstAccelerationIssued
                    .Edit
                    !DemandComplete = Null
                    !DemandWaiting = Null
                    !DemandQueue = Null
                 
                    .Update
                    End With
                    Else
                    MsgBox ("There is no Currrent Wizard Record for this File, Please Contact the IT")
                End If
            Set rstAccelerationIssued = Nothing
            Forms!ForeclosureDetails![AccelerationIssued] = Null
            
                If Not IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails![AccelerationLetter]) Then
                    AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Removed Demand Expires date (" & [AccelerationLetter] & ") by " & GetFullName
                    
                    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
                    strInfo = "Removed Demand Expires date (" & [AccelerationLetter] & ") by " & GetFullName
                    strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
                    strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
                    DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
                    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
                    Forms!Journal.Requery
                    
                    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!AccelerationLetter = Null
                End If
                
                If Forms!ForeclosureDetails!txtClientSentAcceleration = "C" Then
                    AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), ":  Removed C from the Demand Field by " & GetFullName
                    
                    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
                    strInfo = ":  Removed C from the Demand Field by " & GetFullName
                    strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
                    strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
                    DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
                    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
                    Forms!Journal.Requery
                
                    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!txtClientSentAcceleration = ""
                End If
        End If
        Else
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
Else
MsgBox ("The File has dispsotion not buy in or 3rd party, proceduer canceld")
Exit Sub
End If


End Sub

If (IsNull(Disposition) Or (Disposition = 1 Or Disposition = 2)) Then

    If Not IsNull([FairDebt]) Then
        If MsgBox(" You are about to remove dates ? ", vbOKCancel) = vbOK Then
            
            AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Removed Fair Debt (" & [FairDebt] & ") by " & GetFullName
        
            DoCmd.SetWarnings False
            strInfo = "Removed Fair Debt (" & [FairDebt] & ") by " & GetFullName
            strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
            strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!Foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
            DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
            DoCmd.SetWarnings True
            Forms!Journal.Requery
        
            'Put file in FairDebt queue
            Dim rstWFairDebt As Recordset
            Set rstWFairDebt = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * From WizardQueueStats Where FileNumber = " & FileNumber & "And Current = True", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
                If Not rstWFairDebt.EOF Then
                    With rstWFairDebt
                    .Edit
                   ' If IsNull(!RSIIcomplete) Then !RSIIcomplete = #1/1/2011#
                    If Not IsNull(!FairDebtComplete) Then !FairDebtComplete = Null
                    If Not IsNull(!FairDebtWaiting) Then !FairDebtWaiting = Null
                    'If Not IsNull(!NOIcomplete) Then !NOIcomplete = Null
                    '!DateInQueueNOI = Null
                    !AddFair = "Fair"
                  '  If Not IsNull(!RestartQueue) Then !FairDebtRestart = #1/1/2011#
                   .Update
                    End With
                    Else
                    MsgBox ("There is no Currrent Wizard Record for this File, Please Contact the IT")
                End If
            Set rstWFairDebt = Nothing
        
            Forms!ForeclosureDetails![FairDebt] = Null
          
        End If
        Else
        Exit Sub
    End If
Else
MsgBox ("The File has dispsotion not buy in or 3rd party, proceduer canceld")
Exit Sub
End If

End Sub

    If IsNull(NiSiEnd.oldvalue) And Not IsNull(NiSiEnd) Then NameJournal = NameJournal + "Added Ni Si End " & Format(NiSiEnd, "mm/dd/yy") & ". "

Private Sub PurchaserAddress_AfterUpdate()
If Not BHproject Then
Dim strInfo As String
Dim strSQLJournal As String

If checkCmdEdit Then

    If Nz(PurchaserAddress) <> Nz(PurchaserAddress.oldvalue) Then
        If IsNull(PurchaserAddress) And Not IsNull(PurchaserAddress.oldvalue) Then
        MsgBox ("You should put a PurchaserAddress")
        Me.Undo
        Else
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = " Edit Purchaser Address  from " & PurchaserAddress.oldvalue & " To " & PurchaserAddress
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(" & Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber & ", #" & Now & "# , '" & GetFullName() & "', '" & strInfo & "'," & 1 & ")"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
        AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Add PurchaserAddress " & PurchaserAddress
        End If
    End If
Else
    If Not IsNull(PurchaserAddress) Then
            DoCmd.SetWarnings False
            strInfo = " Edit Purchaser Address  from " & PurchaserAddress.oldvalue & " To " & PurchaserAddress
            'strInfo = " Edit Purchaser Address "
            strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
            strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(" & Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FileNumber & ", #" & Now & "# , '" & GetFullName() & "', '" & strInfo & "'," & 1 & ")"
            DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
            DoCmd.SetWarnings True
            Forms!Journal.Requery
            AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Add PurchaserAddress " & PurchaserAddress
    End If

End If

'If Not IsNull(SalePrice) And Not IsNull(Purchaser) And Not IsNull(PurchaserAddress) And Me.PurchaserAddress.Enabled = False Then ComEdit.Enabled = True
End If

End Sub

Private Sub StatusHearing_BeforeUpdate(Cancel As Integer)
If Not BHproject Then
If Not IsNull([StatusHearing]) Then
    If HearingCheking(StatusHearing, 1) = 1 Then
    Cancel = 1
 Else

If Weekday(StatusHearing) = vbSunday Or Weekday(StatusHearing) = vbSaturday Then

    MsgBox "Status Hearing date cannot be Saturday or Sunday", vbCritical
Cancel = 1
Else
Cancel = 0
End If
StatusHearingTime = Null
End If
End If
End If

End Sub

Private Sub StatusHearingTime_AfterUpdate()
If Not BHproject Then

    If IsNull(StatusHearing) Or IsNull(StatusHearingTime) Then Exit Sub
    
'    If Hour(StatusHearingTime) < 8 Or Hour(StatusHearingTime) > 18 Then
'        StatusHearingTime = DateAdd("h", 12, StatusHearingTime)
'        If Hour(StatusHearingTime) < 8 Or Hour(StatusHearingTime) > 18 Then
'            MsgBox "Invalid Status Hearing Time: " & Format$(StatusHearingTime, "h:nn am/pm")
'            ExceptionsHearingTime = Null
'            Exit Sub
'        End If
'    End If

    If Hour(StatusHearingTime) >= 8 And Hour(StatusHearingTime) < 13 Then
        StatusHearingTime = Format$(StatusHearingTime, "h:nn am/pm")
    ElseIf Hour(StatusHearingTime) >= 1 And Hour(StatusHearingTime) <= 6 Then
        StatusHearingTime = DateAdd("h", 12, StatusHearingTime)
    Else
        MsgBox "Hearing time must be between 8:00 AM and 6:00 PM" ': " & Format$(DCHearingTime, "h:nn am/pm")
        StatusHearingTime = Null
        Exit Sub
    End If


    AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Status Hearing scheduled time for " & Format$(StatusHearing, "m/d/yyyy") & " at " & Format$(StatusHearingTime, "h:nn am/pm")
    'If Not IsNull(StatusHearing) Then Call UpdateCalendarStatusHearing
    StatusHearingTime.Locked = True

End If
    'AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Status Hearing scheduled time for " & Format$(StatusHearing, "m/d/yyyy") & " at " & Format$(StatusHearingTime, "h:nn am/pm")
End Sub

                Call DeleteCalendarEvent(StatusHearingEntryID)

Private Sub TitleClaimDate_AfterUpdate()
'AddStatus FileNumber, TitleClaimDate, "Title Claim Needed"
'TitleClaim = True
'Call Visuals
If PrivTitleTab Then
    If Not IsNull(TitleClaimDate) And TitleClaimDate <= Date Then
        AddStatus FileNumber, TitleClaimDate, "Title Claim Needed"
        TitleClaim = True
        Call Visuals
        
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Title claim date"
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery

        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmStatus.Requery
    ElseIf Not IsNull(TitleClaimDate) And TitleClaimDate > Date Then
        MsgBox ("Date can't be in the future")
        TitleClaimDate = ""
    End If
    'added on 9/16/16
    
    If IsNull(TitleClaimDate) Then
        Call UpdateMDSaleSettingWaitingReason(FileNumber, 4)
        
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Title claim date removed"
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    
    End If
Else
MsgBox ("you have no permission to edit")
Me.Undo
End If

End Sub

Private Sub TitleClaimSent2_AfterUpdate()
If PrivTitleTab Then
    If Not IsNull(TitleClaimSent2) Then
    AddStatus FileNumber, TitleClaimSent2, "Sent title claim"
    If IsNull(Comment) Then
        Comment = Format$(Date, "m/d/yyyy") & " Resolved title claim"
    Else
        Comment = Comment & vbNewLine & Format$(Date, "m/d/yyyy") & " Resolved title claim"
    End If
    FeeAmount = DLookup("titleclaim", "clientlist", "clientid=" & Forms![case list]!ClientID)
    If MsgBox("Do you want to override the standard fee of $" & FeeAmount & " for this client?", vbYesNo) = vbYes Then
    FeeAmount = InputBox("Please enter fee, then rememeber to note the journal")
    MsgBox "Please upload fee approval to documents"
    End If
            
    AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-TC", "Title Claim", FeeAmount, 0, True, False, True, True
    
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Sent title claim"
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery

    End If
    Call Visuals
    
    'added on 9/16/16
    If IsNull(TitleClaimSent2) And Not IsNull(TitleClaimSent2.oldvalue) Then
        Call UpdateMDSaleSettingWaitingReason(FileNumber, 4)
        
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Title claim sent date removed"
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    
    End If

Else
MsgBox ("you have no permission to edit")
Me.Undo
End If

Private Sub txtClientSentAcceleration_AfterUpdate()

If Not IsNull(AccelerationLetter) Then
Dim rstJnl As Recordset, ClientSentAccelerationtxt As String
If ClientSentAcceleration = "C" Then
ClientSentAccelerationtxt = "Acceleration Letter noted as sent by client"
Else
ClientSentAcceleration = "Acceleration Letter noted as sent by Rosenberg & Associates"
End If
Set rstJnl = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("select * from journal", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
With rstJnl
.AddNew
!FileNumber = FileNumber
!JournalDate = Now
!Who = GetFullName
!Info = ClientSentAccelerationtxt
!Color = 1
.Update
End With
Set rstJnl = Nothing
End If
AddStatus FileNumber, Date, ClientSentAccelerationtxt
End Sub

Private Sub ClientPaid_AfterUpdate()
If StaffID = 0 Then Call GetLoginName
Me.ReinstateClientPaidStaffID = StaffID
AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Proceeds sent to client"
sfrmDisbursingSurplus.Visible = True
sfrmOriginalSurplus.Visible = True

'Post sale milestone


If Not IsNull(ClientPaid) Then
    Dim InvPct As Double
    Dim cbxClient, LoanType As Integer
    cbxClient = Nz(DLookup("ClientID", "Caselist", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber))
    LoanType = Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1"))
    'Remove SLS on 5/9/18. ticket 3320
    'If Me.DispositionDesc = "3rd party" And cbxClient = 466 Then ' added on 3/9/16 3rd party sale SPS need post sale milestone invoice
'added on 7/6/2018 for 3365 - Nationstar FNMA loans not to invoice the last milestone at Deed recorded but at sale for butin and 3rd party.

If cbxClient = 385 And Me.DispositionDesc = "3rd party" And LoanType = 4 Then
Else
    If Me.DispositionDesc = "3rd party" Then
        
        'Else
             
'            If (Nz(DLookup("MilestoneBilling", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))) = -1 Then
'                If State = "VA" Then
'                    InvPct = DLookup("VAPostsale", "clientlist", "clientid=" & cbxClient)
'                    FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeVAReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
'                ElseIf State = "MD" Then
'                    InvPct = DLookup("MDPostSale", "clientlist", "clientid=" & cbxClient)
'                    FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
'
'                ElseIf State = "DC" Then
'
'                    InvPct = DLookup("DCPostSale", "clientlist", "clientid=" & cbxClient)
'                    FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeDCReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
'
'                End If
'
'            End If
'
'            If InvPct > 0 And FeeAmount > 0 Then
'                AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "Attorney Fee- " & Format(InvPct, "percent") & " at Deed recording of " & Format(FeeAmount, "currency"), InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
'
'            End If


            If State = "MD" Then
                
                If DLookup("MDPostSale", "clientlist", "clientid=" & cbxClient) > 0 Then
                
                    If cbxClient = 634 Then
                        FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
                    Else
                    
                        Select Case Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1"))
                        
                            Case 1 'Conventional
                                FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
                              Case 2 'VA or Veteran's Affairs
                                FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=573")) 'Veteran's Affairs
                              Case 3 'FHA or HUD
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=570")) 'HUD/FHA
                          Case 4
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=177")) 'Fannie Mae
                          Case 5
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=263")) 'Freddie Mac
                          Case Else
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeMDReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
                        End Select
                    End If
                    If (Nz(DLookup("MilestoneBilling", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))) = -1 Then
                            If Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1")) = 4 And cbxClient <> 634 Then
                                InvPct = DLookup("MDPostSale", "clientlist", "clientid=177")
                            Else
                                InvPct = DLookup("MDPostSale", "clientlist", "clientid=" & cbxClient)
                            End If
                    Else
                          InvPct = 1
                    End If
                
                'End If
                        
                    If InvPct > 0 And FeeAmount > 0 Then
                        If Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1")) = 4 And cbxClient <> 634 Then
                                AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "FNMA Attorney Fee- " & Format(InvPct, "percent") & " at Deed recording of " & Format(FeeAmount, "currency"), InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
                        Else
                               AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "Attorney Fee- " & Format(InvPct, "percent") & " at Deed recording of " & Format(FeeAmount, "currency"), InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
                        End If
                    End If
                End If
            End If
            
            
            If State = "VA" Then
            
                If DLookup("VAPostSale", "clientlist", "clientid=" & cbxClient) > 0 Then
            
                    Select Case Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1"))
                    
                        Case 1 'Conventional
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeVAReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
                          Case 2 'VA or Veteran's Affairs
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeVAReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=573")) 'Veteran's Affairs
                          Case 3 'FHA or HUD
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeVAReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=570")) 'HUD/FHA
                          Case 4
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeVAReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=177")) 'Fannie Mae
                          Case 5
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeVAReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=263")) 'Freddie Mac
                          Case Else
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeVAReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
                    End Select
                
                    If (Nz(DLookup("MilestoneBilling", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))) = -1 Then
                            If Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1")) = 4 Then
                                InvPct = DLookup("VAPostsale", "clientlist", "clientid=177")
                            Else
                                InvPct = DLookup("VAPostsale", "clientlist", "clientid=" & cbxClient)
                            End If
                    Else
                          InvPct = 1
                    End If
                
                'End If
                        
                    If InvPct > 0 And FeeAmount > 0 Then
                        If Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1")) = 4 Then
                                AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "FNMA Attorney Fee- " & Format(InvPct, "percent") & " at Deed recording of " & Format(FeeAmount, "currency"), InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
                        Else
                                AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "Attorney Fee- " & Format(InvPct, "percent") & " at Deed recording of " & Format(FeeAmount, "currency"), InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
                    
                        End If
                    End If
                End If
            End If
            
            If State = "DC" Then
                If DLookup("DCPostSale", "clientlist", "clientid=" & cbxClient) > 0 Then
    
                    Select Case Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1"))
                    
                        Case 1 'Conventional
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeDCReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
                          Case 2 'VA or Veteran's Affairs
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeDCReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=573")) 'Veteran's Affairs
                          Case 3 'FHA or HUD
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeDCReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=570")) 'HUD/FHA
                          Case 4
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeDCReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=177")) 'Fannie Mae
                          Case 5
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeDCReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=263")) 'Freddie Mac
                          Case Else
                            FeeAmount = Nz(DLookup("FeeDCReferral", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))
                    End Select
                
                    If (Nz(DLookup("MilestoneBilling", "ClientList", "ClientID=" & cbxClient))) = -1 Then
                            If Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1")) = 4 Then
                                InvPct = DLookup("DCPostsale", "clientlist", "clientid=177")
                            Else
                                InvPct = DLookup("DCPostsale", "clientlist", "clientid=" & cbxClient)
                            End If
                    Else
                          InvPct = 1
                    End If
                
                'End If
                        
                    If InvPct > 0 And FeeAmount > 0 Then
                        If Nz(DLookup("LoanType", "FCDetails", "FileNumber=" & FileNumber & " AND Current=1")) = 4 Then
                                AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "FNMA Attorney Fee- " & Format(InvPct, "percent") & " at Deed recording of " & Format(FeeAmount, "currency"), InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
                        Else
                                AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-REF", "Attorney Fee- " & Format(InvPct, "percent") & " at Deed recording of " & Format(FeeAmount, "currency"), InvPct * FeeAmount, 0, True, True, False, False
                    
                        End If
                    End If
                End If
            End If

            
        'add to need invoice FC
        If InvPct > 0 And FeeAmount > 0 Then
            DoCmd.SetWarnings False
            DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE CaseList set BillCase = True ,BillCaseUpdateUser = " & GetStaffID() & " ,BillCaseUpdateDate = Date() ,BillCaseUpdateReasonID = 35 WHERE [FileNumber] = " & Me.FileNumber)
            DoCmd.SetWarnings True
            
            Dim rstBillReasons As Recordset
            Set rstBillReasons = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * FROM BillingReasonsFCarchive where filenumber=" & FileNumber, dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
            With rstBillReasons
            .AddNew
            !FileNumber = FileNumber
            !BillingReasonID = 35
            !UserID = GetStaffID
            !Date = ClientPaid
            .Update
            End With
        End If
    End If
  End If
End If
End Sub

End If

'If IsNull(MedRequestDate) And IsNull(sfrmLMHearing!Hearing) Then

MsgBox ("Please enter Mediation Request Date or Hearing date before set disposition")
Exit Sub
End If

If IsNull(LMDisposition) And PrivSetDisposition Then
     
    Call SetLMDisposition(0)
    
    If Not CheckCancelDisposition Then
    Exit Sub
    End If
    'Call DeleteFutureHearings(LMDispositionDate)
    Call DeleteFutureHearings(LMDDate)
    Call RemoveSoftHold(FileNumber)
  
  Me.sfrmSoftHold.Requery
  
  'added 1/11/17
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    Dim jnltxt As String
    jnltxt = "Soft Hold mediation Removed and Hold count end as today " & Format(Date, "Short Date")
    strInfo = jnltxt
    strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
    strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(" & FileNumber & ",Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
    DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True

    AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Soft Hold mediation Removed"
    Forms!Journal.Requery
   
End If

'added on 9/13/16 for remove MD SS waiting reason

If Not IsNull(LMDisposition) Then
'Dim rs As Recordset

    Exit Sub

End Sub



Private Sub DateOfDefault_BeforeUpdate(Cancel As Integer)
Cancel = CheckFutureDate(DateOfDefault)
If (Cancel = 1) Then Exit Sub

If Not IsNull(DateOfDefault) Then
  If (Not IsNull(Me.LastPaymentApplied)) Then
  
    If (DateDiff("d", DateOfDefault, LastPaymentApplied) >= 1) Then
    
        Cancel = 1
        MsgBox "Date must be on or after Last Payment Applied.", vbCritical
    End If
  End If
  
End If
End Sub

Private Sub DeedAppReceived_DblClick(Cancel As Integer)
If FileReadOnly Or EditDispute Then
   DoCmd.CancelEvent
Else
    DeedAppReceived = Date
    Me.DocBackDOA = True
    AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Substitution of Trustee Received"
    
        Dim clientShor As String
        Dim strInsert As String
        clientShor = DLookup("ShortClientName", "ClientList", "ClientID= " & Forms![case list]!ClientID)
        clientShor = Replace(clientShor, "'", "''")
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInsert = "Insert Into TrackingSOTreceived (CaseFile,ProjectName,ClientShortName,Client,DIT,DeedAppReceived,StaffID,StaffName,state) Values (" & FileNumber & ",'" & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & "','" & clientShor & "', " & Forms![case list]!ClientID & ", #" & Now() & "#,#" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!DeedAppReceived & "#, " & GetStaffID & ",'" & GetFullName() & "','" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!State & "')"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strInsert
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        clientShor = ""
        strInsert = ""
    
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    strInfo = "Received Substitution of Trustee by " & GetFullName
    strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
    strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
    DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
    Forms!Journal.Requery
End If

End Sub

Private Sub DeedAppSentToRecord_AfterUpdate()
 Dim clientShor As String
 Dim strInsert As String
If BHproject Then
    If Not (IsNull(DeedAppSentToRecord)) Then
    AddStatus FileNumber, DeedAppSentToRecord, "Substitution of Trustee sent to record"
      sfrmStatus.Requery
        clientShor = DLookup("ShortClientName", "ClientList", "ClientID= " & Forms![case list]!ClientID)
        clientShor = Replace(clientShor, "'", "''")
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInsert = "Insert Into TrackingSOTSentToRecord (CaseFile,ProjectName,ClientShortName,Client,DIT,DeedAppSentToRecord,StaffID,StaffName,state) Values (" & FileNumber & ",'" & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & "','" & clientShor & "', " & Forms![case list]!ClientID & ", #" & Now() & "#,#" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!DeedAppSentToRecord & "#, " & GetStaffID & ",'" & GetFullName() & "','" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!State & "')"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strInsert
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        clientShor = ""
        strInsert = ""
            
    
    
    Exit Sub
    End If

Else
        If Not (IsNull(DeedAppSentToRecord)) Then
        AddStatus FileNumber, DeedAppSentToRecord, "Substitution of Trustee sent to record"
       sfrmStatus.Requery
        clientShor = DLookup("ShortClientName", "ClientList", "ClientID= " & Forms![case list]!ClientID)
        clientShor = Replace(clientShor, "'", "''")
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInsert = "Insert Into TrackingSOTSentToRecord (CaseFile,ProjectName,ClientShortName,Client,DIT,DeedAppSentToRecord,StaffID,StaffName,state) Values (" & FileNumber & ",'" & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & "','" & clientShor & "', " & Forms![case list]!ClientID & ", #" & Now() & "#,#" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!DeedAppSentToRecord & "#, " & GetStaffID & ",'" & GetFullName() & "','" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!State & "')"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strInsert
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        clientShor = ""
        strInsert = ""
          If State = "VA" Then
        DoCmd.OpenForm "GetPostage", , , , , acDialog, "Enter total Overnight costs|FC-SOT|SOT Overnight Delivery Costs"
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-SOT", "Substitution of Trustees Mailing", Nz(DLookup("Value", "StandardCharges", "ID=" & 1)), 76, False, True, False, True
          End If
        End If
End If

End Sub

Private Sub DismissalDate_AfterUpdate()
    
             
If MsgBox("Do you want to dismiss the case? ", vbYesNo) = vbYes Then
 AddStatus FileNumber, DismissalDate, "Case " & [CourtCaseNumber] & " Dismissed"
    'CaseNuUpdate = True
    
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & "Case " & [CourtCaseNumber] & " Dismissed" & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
              
    'Call RemoveCaseFiled
    
     
      'Filing Fee
      AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Oth", "Filing Fee for Dismissal", 15, 187, False, False, False, True
      'Overnight costs
      AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Oth", "Overnight costs for Dismissal", 7, 77, False, False, False, True

Else
    
    If IsNull(DismissalDate.oldvalue) Then
        DismissalDate = ""
    Else
        DismissalDate = DismissalDate.oldvalue
    End If

End If

End Sub

Private Sub DispositionRescinded_AfterUpdate()

If Not IsNull(DispositionRescinded) Then
Forms![case list]!BillCase = True
Forms![case list]!BillCaseUpdateUser = GetStaffID()
Forms![case list]!BillCaseUpdateDate = Date
Forms![case list]![BillCaseUpdateReasonID] = 6
Forms![case list]!lblBilling.Visible = True
Forms![case list].SetFocus
DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord
Forms![ForeclosureDetails].SetFocus

Dim rstBillReasons As Recordset
Set rstBillReasons = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("Select * FROM BillingReasonsFCarchive where filenumber=" & FileNumber, dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
With rstBillReasons
.AddNew
!FileNumber = FileNumber
!BillingReasonID = 6
!UserID = GetStaffID
!Date = DispositionRescinded
.Update
End With

If Not IsNull(DispositionRescinded) And RescindClientReq = True Then

'added on 8/14/18 for Litigation NTI

    
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        DoCmd.RunSQL ("Insert Into BillingReasonsFCarchive (FileNumber, BillingReasonID, UserID, [Date]) Values (" & FileNumber & ", 69, " & GetStaffID & ",# " & DispositionRescinded & " #)")
        DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE CaseList set BillCase = True ,BillCaseUpdateUser = " & GetStaffID() & " ,BillCaseUpdateDate = Date() ,BillCaseUpdateReasonID = 69 WHERE [FileNumber] = " & FileNumber)
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
End If



AddStatus FileNumber, DispositionRescinded, "Disposition Rescinded"
AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC", "Disposition Rescinded- Placeholder entry", 0, 0, True, False, False, False
End If
End Sub

Private Sub DocBackAff7105_AfterUpdate()
If Me.Dirty Then DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord
If DocBackAff7105 Then
    AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Received Affidavit Pursuant to MD Real Property Code 7-105.1(D)(II)"
    
    If Not DocBackAff7105 Then
           DocBackAff7105 = True
           If Me.Dirty Then DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord
    End If
    
Else
    AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Removed Affidavit Pursuant to MD Real Property Code 7-105.1(D)(II)"
    
    If DocBackAff7105 Then
           DocBackAff7105 = False
        If Me.Dirty Then DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord
    End If
End If

End Sub

Private Sub DocBackDOA_AfterUpdate()
If Me.Dirty Then DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord

    If DocBackDOA Then
        DeedAppReceived = Date
        AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Received Substitution of Trustee"
        
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Received Substitution of Trustee by " & GetFullName
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
        
            Dim clientShor As String
            Dim strInsert As String
            clientShor = DLookup("ShortClientName", "ClientList", "ClientID= " & Forms![case list]!ClientID)
            clientShor = Replace(clientShor, "'", "''")
            DoCmd.SetWarnings False
            strInsert = "Insert Into TrackingSOTreceived (CaseFile,ProjectName,ClientShortName,Client,DIT,DeedAppReceived,StaffID,StaffName,state) Values (" & FileNumber & ",'" & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & "','" & clientShor & "', " & Forms![case list]!ClientID & ", #" & Now() & "#,#" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!DeedAppReceived & "#, " & GetStaffID & ",'" & GetFullName() & "','" & Forms![ForeclosureDetails]!State & "')"
            DoCmd.RunSQL strInsert
            DoCmd.SetWarnings True
            clientShor = ""
            strInsert = ""
        If Not DocBackDOA Then
           DocBackDOA = True
           If Me.Dirty Then DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord
        End If
    Else
        DeedAppReceived = Null
        AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Removed Substitution of Trustee"
    
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        strInfo = "Removed Substitution of Trustee by " & GetFullName
        strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
        strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(Forms!foreclosuredetails!FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
        DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        Forms!Journal.Requery
    
        If DocBackDOA Then
           DocBackDOA = False
           If Me.Dirty Then DoCmd.RunCommand acCmdSaveRecord
        End If
    End If
End Sub
