'DC POST SALE 12/1/16 - Lin - Transfer Tax/Deed recording filing fee, Recordation Tax,ROS filing fee,Audit Filing fee and Release Lis Pendens for buy ins
        Dim Baseprice1 As Currency
        Dim Baseprice2 As Currency
        Dim RecordationBasePrice, RecordationBasePrice1 As Currency
        Dim OccupStatus As Integer
        
'updated on 2/22/2017

    If SelectedDispositionID = 1 Then
    
        If Me.State = "DC" And IsNull(OccupancyStatusID) Then
            MsgBox ("Occupancy Status is missing")
            CheckCancelDisposition = False
        Exit Sub
        End If
    
        If Me.State = "DC" And (IsNull(AssessedValue) Or AssessedValue = "") Then
            MsgBox ("Assessed Value is missing")
            CheckCancelDisposition = False
        Exit Sub
        End If
        
'Forms!ForeclosureDetails.Requery
        If SalePrice <= AssessedValue * 30 / 100 Then
            RecordationBasePrice = AssessedValue
        Else
            RecordationBasePrice = SalePrice
        End If
            
        OccupStatus = OccupancyStatusID.Column(0)
        
        'RecordationBasePrice = Baseprice1 * 1.1 / 100 + Baseprice2 * 1.45 / 100
        Select Case LoanType.Column(0)
    
        Case 1
            If OccupStatus = 5 Then
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 1.45 / 100
            ElseIf RecordationBasePrice >= 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 1.45 / 100
            ElseIf OccupStatus <> 5 And RecordationBasePrice < 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 1.1 / 100
            
            End If
            
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Recordation Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Transfer Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
        Case 2 ' VA
            If OccupStatus = 5 Then
                RecordationBasePrice1 = RecordationBasePrice * 0.725 / 100
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 1.45 / 100
                
            ElseIf RecordationBasePrice >= 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice1 = RecordationBasePrice * 0.725 / 100
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 1.45 / 100
                
            ElseIf OccupStatus <> 5 And RecordationBasePrice < 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice1 = RecordationBasePrice * 0.55 / 100
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 1.1 / 100
                
            End If
            
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Recordation Tax (Trustee to Servicer)", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Transfer Tax (Trustee to Servicer)", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
            
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Recordation Tax (Servicer to VA)", Format(RecordationBasePrice1, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Transfer Tax (Servicer to VA)", Format(RecordationBasePrice1, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
         
        Case 3 'HUD
        
            If OccupStatus = 5 Then
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 1.45 / 100
                
            ElseIf RecordationBasePrice >= 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 1.45 / 100
            ElseIf OccupStatus <> 5 And RecordationBasePrice < 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 1.1 / 100
            
            End If
            
            If OccupStatus = 5 Then
                RecordationBasePrice1 = AssessedValue * 0.725 / 100
                
            ElseIf AssessedValue >= 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice1 = AssessedValue * 0.725 / 100
            ElseIf OccupStatus <> 5 And AssessedValue < 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice1 = AssessedValue * 0.55 / 100
            
            End If
            
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC First Recordation Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC First Transfer Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
            
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Second Recordation Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice1, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Second Transfer Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice1, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True

        
        Case 4, 5
            If OccupStatus = 5 Then
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 0.725 / 100
      
            ElseIf RecordationBasePrice >= 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 0.725 / 100
            ElseIf OccupStatus <> 5 And RecordationBasePrice < 400000 Then
                RecordationBasePrice = RecordationBasePrice * 0.55 / 100
            End If
            
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Recordation Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "DC Transfer Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
            
        End Select
'        If SalePrice > 400000 Then
'            Baseprice1 = 400000
'            Baseprice2 = SalePrice - 400000
'        Else
'            Baseprice1 = SalePrice
'        End If
        
'        RecordationBasePrice = Baseprice1 * 1.1 / 100 + Baseprice2 * 1.45 / 100
        'If SelectedDispositionID = 1 Then
        'AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Recordation Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
        'AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Transfer Tax", Format(RecordationBasePrice, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Deed recording filing fee", 31.5, 187, False, False, False, True
        'AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Audit filing fee", 37.05, 187, False, False, False, True - 8/7/17 per diane, remove auto charge, invoice when do the work. tkt 2992
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Release Lis Pendens", 31.5, 0, False, False, False, True
        'AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-RPT", "ROS filing fee", 16.45, 0, False, False, False, True - 8/7/17 per diane, remove auto charge, invoice when do the work. tkt 2992

    End If

          
        If SelectedDispositionID = 2 Then
        
            'AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Rider Bond", Format(SalePrice * 0.004, "currency"), 0, False, False, False, True

If Jurisdiction = 17 Then
    Dim RecordationTax As Currency
       
    If SalePrice >= 500000 Then
'        RecordationTax = 500000 * DLookup("RecordationTaxMD", "JurisdictionList", "jurisdictionid=" & Jurisdiction) / 1000
'        RecordationTax = RecordationTax + (SalePrice - 500000) * 1.35 / 100
    
    
        RecordationTax = (-1000 * Int(500000 / -1000)) * DLookup("RecordationTaxMD", "JurisdictionList", "jurisdictionid=" & Jurisdiction) / 1000
        RecordationTax = RecordationTax + (-1000 * Int(SalePrice - 500000) / -1000) * 1.35 / 100

    Else
        'RecordationTax = SalePrice * DLookup("RecordationTaxMD", "JurisdictionList", "jurisdictionid=" & Jurisdiction) / 1000
        
        RecordationTax = (-1000 * Int(SalePrice / -1000)) * DLookup("RecordationTaxMD", "JurisdictionList", "jurisdictionid=" & Jurisdiction) / 1000
        

    End If
    
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Recordation Tax", RecordationTax, 313, False, False, False, True
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "State Transfer Tax", (SalePrice * DLookup("StateTransferTaxMD", "JurisdictionList", "jurisdictionid=" & Jurisdiction)) / 100, 187, False, False, False, True
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "County Transfer Tax", SalePrice / 100, 313, False, False, False, True
Else

    AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Recordation Tax", Int(SalePrice / 500 + 0.999) * DLookup("RecordationTaxMD", "JurisdictionList", "jurisdictionid=" & Jurisdiction), 187, False, False, False, True
    AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "State Transfer Tax", (SalePrice * DLookup("StateTransferTaxMD", "JurisdictionList", "jurisdictionid=" & Jurisdiction)) / 100, 187, False, False, False, True
End If

    'added on 2/15/17 for Washington County, MD county transfer tax
    If Jurisdiction = 23 Then
        Dim CountyTransfer As Double
        
        If SalePrice < 50000 Then CountyTransfer = 0
        If SalePrice = 50000 Then CountyTransfer = SalePrice
        If SalePrice > 50000 Then CountyTransfer = (SalePrice - 50000)
           
        If CountyTransfer > 0 Then
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "County Transfer Tax", (CountyTransfer * DLookup("CountyTransferTaxMD", "JurisdictionList", "jurisdictionid=" & Jurisdiction)) / 100, 187, False, False, False, True
        End If
    Else
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "County Transfer Tax", (SalePrice * DLookup("CountyTransferTaxMD", "JurisdictionList", "jurisdictionid=" & Jurisdiction)) / 100, 187, False, False, False, True
        
    End If

        .MoveFirst

    End If

        DoCmd.OpenForm "EditBKDataFromFCDispostionBk", , , "FileNumber = " & FileNumber
        
               
    End If
    If CaseTypeID = 8 And Nz(SaleCompleted) = 0 Then    ' Monitor Sale cancelled
        If MsgBox("Do you want to change this file to Foreclosure?", vbYesNo + vbDefaultButton2) = vbYes Then
         'sarabalani      5/12/15    CaseTypeID = 1
        DoCmd.SetWarnings False
        DoCmd.RunSQL ("UPDATE CaseList set CaseTypeID = 1 WHERE [FileNumber] = " & Me.FileNumber)
        DoCmd.SetWarnings True
        
 
        End If
    End If
 
'Virginia
    
If (State = "VA") Then
    Dim varFeeAmt As Variant
    Dim currAmt As Currency
    
    If Disposition = 1 Then
    
    'Deed costs for buy ins
        If LoanType = 4 Or LoanType = 5 Then
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Deed Recordation", 23, 187, False, False, False, True
        Else
            AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Tax", "Deed Recordation", 43, 187, False, False, False, True
        End If
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Deed", "Record Deed- Overnight Costs", 7, 77, False, False, False, False
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Deed", "Receipt of Recorded Deed Postage", Nz(DLookup("Value", "StandardCharges", "ID=" & 1)), 76, False, True, False, False
                
                'calc 1% Trustee commission
        If Not IsNull(SalePrice) And LoanType = 1 Then
            If DLookup("TrusteeComm", "JurisdictionList", "JurisdictionID=" & Jurisdiction) = True Then
                FeeAmount = SalePrice * 0.01
                If FeeAmount > 0 Then
                    AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-COMM", "Trustees Commission to Commonwealth Trustees", FeeAmount, 0, False, True, False, False
                End If
            End If
        End If
    End If

    If SelectedDispositionID < 3 Then 'Buyin and 3rd party fees/costs
        'JPM SCRA  - **recode, needs to be per party
        If Forms![case list]!ClientID = 97 Then
          Set rstNames = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("SELECT Names.FileNumber, Names.mortgagor, Names.First, Names.Last, Names.SSN FROM [Names] GROUP BY Names.FileNumber, Names.mortgagor, Names.First, Names.Last, Names.SSN HAVING (((Names.FileNumber)=" & FileNumber & ") AND ((Names.mortgagor)=Yes) AND ((Names.SSN) Is Not Null)) OR (((Names.FileNumber)=" & FileNumber & ") AND ((Names.mortgagor)=Yes) AND ((Names.SSN)<>""999999999""))", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
              With rstNames
              .MoveLast
              ctr = .RecordCount
              .MoveFirst
              End With
          Cost = ctr * DLookup("ivalue", "db", "ID=" & 32)
          AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-DOD", "DOD Search- JPM Post Sale", Cost, 0, True, True, False, False
          AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-DOD", "DOD Search- JPM Deed", Cost, 0, True, True, False, False
        End If
        'Title Update
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-Title", "Title update- post sale", 55, 0, False, False, False, True
        'Auditor Fee
            Dim VAAuditorFee As Currency
            If (IsNull(SalePrice)) Then
              MsgBox "Sales price is missing. Auditor Fee was not added to the billing sheet.", vbCritical
            Else
              VAAuditorFee = CalculateVAAuditorFee(SalePrice)
              AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-AUD", "Commissioner of Accounts", VAAuditorFee, 188, False, False, False, True
            End If
            
        'LNA cost
        If (DocBackLostNote = True) And (DocBackOrigNote = False) Then
               AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-AUD", "LNA to Commissioner ", DLookup("costsLostnoteaudit", "clientlist", "clientid=" & Forms![case list]!ClientID), 188, False, False, False, False
        End If
            
        'DoCmd.OpenForm "GetPostage", , , , , acDialog, "Enter overnight costs to the Commissioner|FC-AUD|Overnight Costs to Commissioner"
        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-AUD", "Return mail postage for fee audit", 1.5, 76, False, True, False, False  'set as $1.50 true up later
        'Prompt for Liens/Property taxes
        If MsgBox("Are there liens or real property taxes to enter?") = vbYes Then
        DoCmd.OpenForm "GetFeeNew", , , , , acDialog, "Enter Total Amount of Liens & Property Taxes Paid|FC-TAX|Liens and Property Taxes|"
        End If
    End If
End If

'---VA end
'3rd party
If SelectedDispositionID = 2 Then
'calc 5% Trustee commission
            If Not IsNull(SalePrice) And LoanType = 1 Then
                If DLookup("TrusteeComm", "JurisdictionList", "JurisdictionID=" & Jurisdiction) = True Then
                    FeeAmount = SalePrice * 0.05
                    If FeeAmount > 0 Then
                        AddInvoiceItem FileNumber, "FC-COMM", "Trustees Commission to Commonwealth Trustees (less all attorney fees and co-counsel fees)*", FeeAmount, 0, False, True, False, False
                    End If
                End If
            End If
End If

  Call Visuals
End If

    Dim StrDis As String

    DoCmd.RunSQL strInsert
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
End If

    End If
    cmdClose.SetFocus
    cmdSetLMDisposition.Enabled = False ' don't allow any changes
    
   
    DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    DoCmd.RunSQL ("update FCdetails set LMDisposition = " & SelectedDispositionID & ", LMDispositionStaffID = " & StaffID & ", LMDispositionDate = Now() where [FileNumber] = " & Me.FileNumber & " and current=true")
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
    
    LMD = SelectedDispositionID
    LMDDate = Date

    LMDispositionDesc.Requery
    AddStatus FileNumber, Date, "Add Mediation Disposition"
    'StatusText = Nz(DLookup("LMDisposition", "LMDisposition", "LMDispositionID=" & LMDisposition))
    StatusText = Nz(DLookup("LMDisposition", "LMDisposition", "LMDispositionID= " & LMD))
    If StatusText <> "" Then AddStatus FileNumber, Now(), "Added Mediation Disposition " & StatusText & " "
    
    Call Visuals
    DoCmd.OpenForm "SetLMTrustee", , , , , acDialog
    
End If

Private Sub UpdateCalendar()

Dim emailGroup As String
'If IsNull(SaleCalendarEntryID) Then Exit Sub 'sarab

If Nz(SaleCalendarEntryID) = "X" Then Exit Sub

If IsNull(Sale) And Not IsNull(SaleCalendarEntryID) Then
    Call DeleteCalendarEvent(SaleCalendarEntryID)
    SaleCalendarEntryID = Null
    Exit Sub
End If
'DLookup("ShortClientName", "qryClientAddress")

'getTrustees(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!lstTrustees, Forms!ForeclosureDetails!lstTrustees)

If Forms![case list]!CaseTypeID = 8 Then
    emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipMO"
    
    If Nz(SaleCalendarEntryID) = "" Then   ' new event on calendar
    SaleCalendarEntryID = AddCalendarEvent(Sale + Nz(SaleTime, 0), IsNull(SaleTime), getTrustees(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!lstTrustees, Forms!ForeclosureDetails!lstTrustees) & " v. " & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & " (" & FileNumber & ") SR SALE", Forms![case list]!JurisdictionID.Column(1), 9, emailGroup)
    Else                                    ' change existing event on calendar
        Call UpdateCalendarEvent(SaleCalendarEntryID, Sale + Nz(SaleTime, 0), IsNull(SaleTime), getTrustees(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!lstTrustees, Forms!ForeclosureDetails!lstTrustees) & " v. " & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & " (" & FileNumber & ") SR SALE", Forms![case list]!JurisdictionID.Column(1), 9)
    End If


Else
    Select Case State
    
    Case "MD"
    emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC-MD"
    Case "DC"
    emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC-DC"
    Case "VA"
    emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC-VA"
    Case Else
    emailGroup = "SharedCalRecip"
    End Select


    If Nz(SaleCalendarEntryID) = "" Then   ' new event on calendar
        SaleCalendarEntryID = AddCalendarEvent(Sale + Nz(SaleTime, 0), IsNull(SaleTime), DLookup("ShortClientName", "qryClientAddress") & " v. " & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & " (" & FileNumber & ")", Forms![case list]!JurisdictionID.Column(1), 1, emailGroup)
    Else                                    ' change existing event on calendar
        Call UpdateCalendarEvent(SaleCalendarEntryID, Sale + Nz(SaleTime, 0), IsNull(SaleTime), DLookup("ShortClientName", "qryClientAddress") & " v. " & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & " (" & FileNumber & ")", Forms![case list]!JurisdictionID.Column(1), 1)
    End If
End If

End Sub

Private Sub DeleteFutureHearings(pDispositionDate As Date)

Dim rstHearings As Recordset
Dim i As Integer

Set rstHearings = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM LMHearings WHERE FileNumber=" & Me!FileNumber & " AND datediff('d',#" & pDispositionDate & "#, Hearing) > 0", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)

With rstHearings

  If Not .BOF Then
    .MoveFirst
    Do While Not .EOF
  
      If (Not IsNull(rstHearings![HearingCalendarEntryID])) Then
      
          DeleteCalendarEvent (rstHearings![HearingCalendarEntryID])
      End If
  
      .Delete
      .MoveNext
    Loop
  End If
  
  .Close
End With

Me.sfrmLMHearing.Requery


End Sub

Private Sub cmdShowCalendarData_Click()

On Error GoTo Err_cmdShowCalendarData_Click
If Len(Nz(SaleCalendarEntryID)) > 2 Then Call CalendarEventInfo(SaleCalendarEntryID)

Exit_cmdShowCalendarData_Click:
    Exit Sub

Err_cmdShowCalendarData_Click:
    MsgBox Err.Description
    Resume Exit_cmdShowCalendarData_Click
    
End Sub

Private Sub UpdateCalendarExceptionHearing()

Dim emailGroup As String

If Nz(ExceptionsHearingEntryID) = "X" Then Exit Sub

If IsNull(ExceptionsHearing) And Not IsNull(ExceptionsHearingEntryID) Then
    Call DeleteCalendarEvent(ExceptionsHearingEntryID)
    ExceptionsHearingEntryID = Null
    Exit Sub
End If

Select Case State
Case "MD"
'emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC-MD"
emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC_MDStatus/ExceptionHearings"
Case "DC"
emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC-DC"
Case "VA"
emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC-VA"
Case Else
emailGroup = "SharedCalRecip"
End Select

If Nz(ExceptionsHearingEntryID) = "" Then   ' new event on calendar
    ExceptionsHearingEntryID = AddCalendarEvent(ExceptionsHearing + Nz(ExceptionsHearingTime, 0), IsNull(ExceptionsHearingTime), DLookup("ShortClientName", "qryClientAddress") & " v. " & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & " Exception Hearing " & " (" & FileNumber & ")", Forms![case list]!JurisdictionID.Column(1), 8, emailGroup)
Else                                    ' change existing event on calendar
    Call UpdateCalendarEvent(ExceptionsHearingEntryID, ExceptionsHearing + Nz(ExceptionsHearingTime, 0), IsNull(ExceptionsHearingTime), DLookup("ShortClientName", "qryClientAddress") & " v. " & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & " Exception Hearing " & " (" & FileNumber & ")", Forms![case list]!JurisdictionID.Column(1), 8)
End If
    
End Sub


Private Sub UpdateCalendarStatusHearing()

Dim emailGroup As String

If Nz(StatusHearingEntryID) = "X" Then Exit Sub

If IsNull(StatusHearing) And Not IsNull(StatusHearingEntryID) Then
    Call DeleteCalendarEvent(StatusHearingEntryID)
    StatusHearingEntryID = Null
    Exit Sub
End If

Select Case State
Case "MD"
'emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC-MD"
emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC_MDStatus/ExceptionHearings"

Case "DC"
emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC-DC"
Case "VA"
emailGroup = "SharedCalRecipFC-VA"
Case Else
emailGroup = "SharedCalRecip"
End Select

If Nz(StatusHearingEntryID) = "" And Not IsNull(StatusHearing) And Not IsNull(StatusHearingTime) Then   ' new event on calendar
    StatusHearingEntryID = AddCalendarEvent(StatusHearing + Nz(StatusHearingTime, 0), IsNull(StatusHearingTime), DLookup("ShortClientName", "qryClientAddress") & " v. " & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & " Status Hearing " & " (" & FileNumber & ")", Forms![case list]!JurisdictionID.Column(1), 8, emailGroup)
Else                                    ' change existing event on calendar
    Call UpdateCalendarEvent(StatusHearingEntryID, StatusHearing + Nz(StatusHearingTime, 0), IsNull(StatusHearingTime), DLookup("ShortClientName", "qryClientAddress") & " v. " & Forms![case list]!PrimaryDefName & " Status Hearing " & " (" & FileNumber & ")", Forms![case list]!JurisdictionID.Column(1), 8)
End If
    
End Sub

Function HasNotNumber(strData As String) As Boolean
    Dim iCnt As Integer

    For iCnt = 1 To Len(strData)
        If Not IsNumeric(Mid(strData, iCnt, 1)) Then
            HasNotNumber = True
            Exit Function
        End If
    Next iCnt

End Function

Private Sub SetDCAtty()
Dim i, j, t As Integer
Dim rst, rst1 As Recordset

Set rst = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("select * from DC_CompSelectedAtty where filenumber = " & Forms![case list]!FileNumber, dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)

    If Not rst.EOF Then
        Do Until rst.EOF
            For i = 0 To lstDCAtty.ListCount - 1
        
                If rst!AttyID = Val(lstDCAtty.Column(0, i)) Then
                    If Not lstDCAtty.Selected(i) Then
                        lstDCAtty.Selected(i) = True
                    End If
                End If
                Next i
                    rst.MoveNext
                Loop
        
                'cmdConfirm.Enabled = False
                cmdConfirm.Visible = False
                
            rst.Close
            Set rst = Nothing
    Else
        rst.Close
        Set rst = Nothing
                'lstDCAtty.Locked = False
                'cmdConfirm.Enabled = True
                'cmdConfirm.Visible = True
            
            DoCmd.SetWarnings False
            
            Set rst1 = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("select ID,Name,DCBar,Email from Staff where ID in (135,788,400) ", dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
            
            Do Until rst1.EOF
                DoCmd.RunSQL ("Insert into DC_CompSelectedAtty (Filenumber,AttyID,Name,DCBar,Email) Values(" & Me.FileNumber & "," & rst1!ID & ",'" & rst1!Name & "'," & rst1!DCBar & ", '" & rst1!EMail & "')")
            rst1.MoveNext
            Loop
            
            DoCmd.SetWarnings True
            rst1.Close
            Set rst1 = Nothing
            
            Set rst = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset("select * from DC_CompSelectedAtty where filenumber = " & Me.FileNumber, dbOpenDynaset, dbSeeChanges)
                            
            Do Until rst.EOF
           
            For i = 0 To lstDCAtty.ListCount - 1

                If rst!AttyID = Val(lstDCAtty.Column(0, i)) Then
                    If Not lstDCAtty.Selected(i) Then
                        lstDCAtty.Selected(i) = True
                    End If
                End If
                Next i
                    rst.MoveNext
                Loop
            rst.Close
            Set rst = Nothing
    End If

Private Sub ServiceChangeTrack()
Dim Journal1, Journal2 As String

If chMannerofService = True And P_Old = False Then
    Journal2 = "Personally"
ElseIf chMannerofService = False And P_Old = True Then
    Journal1 = "Manner Service changed from Personally to "
ElseIf chMannerofService = P_Old Then
End If

If Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMannerService!SubstituteService = True And S_Old = False Then
    Journal2 = "Substitute"
ElseIf Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMannerService!SubstituteService = False And S_Old = True Then
    Journal1 = "Manner Service changed from via Substitute to "
ElseIf Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMannerService!SubstituteService = S_Old Then
End If

If Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMannerService!PostingMailingService = True And M_Old = False Then
    Journal2 = "Posting and Mailing"
ElseIf Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMannerService!PostingMailingService = False And M_Old = True Then
    Journal1 = "Manner Service changed from Posting and Mailing to "
ElseIf Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMannerService!PostingMailingService = M_Old Then
End If

strInfo = Journal1 + Journal2

If Len(Journal1) <> 0 And Len(Journal2) > 0 Then

    AddStatus FileNumber, Date, strInfo
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmStatus.Requery

DoCmd.SetWarnings False
    'strinfo = Journal1 + Journal2
    strInfo = Replace(strInfo, "'", "''")
    strSQLJournal = "Insert into Journal (FileNumber,JournalDate,Who,Info,Color) Values(FileNumber,Now,GetFullName(),'" & strInfo & "',1 )"
    DoCmd.RunSQL strSQLJournal
    DoCmd.SetWarnings True
    Journal1 = ""
    Journal2 = ""
    strInfo = ""
Forms!Journal.Requery
End If

P_Old = False
S_Old = False
M_Old = False

P_Old = chMannerofService
S_Old = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMannerService!SubstituteService
M_Old = Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmMannerService!PostingMailingService

End Sub

dcheck = False
          If WizardSource = "ServiceMailed" Then
            If IsNull(ServiceMailed) Then
                Me.ServiceMailed = Now()
                dcheck = True
            End If
          Else
            Me.Undo
          End If
End Sub

Private Sub SetlossMitResponsibility()
Me.FairDebtDispute.Locked = False

Me.ReinstatementSent.Locked = False
Me.PayoffRequested.Locked = False
Me.PayoffSent.Locked = False
Me.SimultaneousForeclosure.Locked = False
Me.ForebearanceAgreementReceived.Locked = False
Me.ForebearanceAgreementSend.Locked = False
Me.TitleOrder_LossMit.Locked = False
Me.TitleDue_LossMit.Locked = False
Me.TitleBack_LossMit.Locked = False
Me.TitleThru_LossMit.Locked = False
Me.chTitleClaim_LostMit.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.DILSentBorrowers.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.DILReceivedBorrowers.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.DILSentClient.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.DILReceivedClient.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.DILInstructionstoRecord.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.DILSentRecord.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.DILRecorded.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.DILReferralReceived.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.TitleClearforDIL.Locked = False
Me.sfrmFCDIL.Form.DILCancelled.Locked = False

Private Sub LockLoanInfo()
    If Not IsNull(DOTdate) Then DOTdate.Locked = True
        If Not IsNull(DOTdate) Then DOTdate.Locked = True
        If Not IsNull(OriginalTrustee) Then OriginalTrustee.Locked = True
        If Not IsNull(OriginalBeneficiary) Then OriginalBeneficiary.Locked = True
        If Not IsNull(OriginalMortgagors) Then OriginalMortgagors.Locked = True
        If Not IsNull(OriginalPBal) Then OriginalPBal.Locked = True
        If Not IsNull(RemainingPBal) Then RemainingPBal.Locked = True
        If Not IsNull(Liber) Then Liber.Locked = True
        If Not IsNull(Folio) Then Folio.Locked = True
        If Not IsNull(DOTrecorded) Then DOTrecorded.Locked = True
        
        DOT.Locked = True

    Me.sfrmMERS!chMers.Locked = True

End Sub
Private Sub SWDSwichOn()

'FinalPkg
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!FTPRejectionrcvd.Locked = False
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseDeadline.Locked = False
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseSent.Locked = False
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FinalPkg.Locked = False

    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!FTPRejectionrcvd.Enabled = True
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseDeadline.Enabled = True
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseSent.Enabled = True
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FinalPkg.Enabled = True
  
    If Not IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!FTPRejectionrcvd) Then
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!FTPRejectionrcvd.Locked = True
    End If
    
    If Not IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseDeadline) Then
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseDeadline.Locked = True
    End If
    
    If Not IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseSent) Then
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseSent.Locked = True
    End If
    
    If Not IsNull(Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FinalPkg) Then
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FinalPkg.Locked = True
    End If
    
    If LoanType = 3 Then
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!Conveyancedate.Locked = False
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!Conveyancedate.Enabled = True
    Else
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!Conveyancedate.Locked = False
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!Conveyancedate.Enabled = False
    End If
    
End Sub


Private Sub SWDSwichOff()

    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!FTPRejectionrcvd.Locked = False
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseDeadline.Locked = False
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseSent.Locked = False
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FinalPkg.Locked = False


    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!FTPRejectionrcvd.Enabled = False
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseDeadline.Enabled = False
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!ResponseSent.Enabled = False
    Forms!ForeclosureDetails!FinalPkg.Enabled = False

    
    If LoanType = 3 Then
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!Conveyancedate.Locked = False
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!Conveyancedate.Enabled = True
    Else
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!Conveyancedate.Locked = False
        Forms!ForeclosureDetails!sfrmSWDConvDate!Conveyancedate.Enabled = False
    End If

End Sub
